            Our certifications are offered instantly online and/or via mail
           </li>
           <li>
            Print the Certificate and wallet size Card or have it mailed, click
            <a class="visited_hyperlink" href="http://ecprcertification.com/index.php/page/certificate_sample/" target="_blank">
             <strong>
              here
             </strong>
            </a>
            for sample
           </li>
          </ul>
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td>
          <p class="heading_index" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
           What are Experts saying?
          </p>
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td>
          <ul>
           <li>
            In November of 2005, a group of leading medical researchers from top Universities across North America performed a marquee study using employees from American Airlines. The study conclusively showed that 20 minute course in CPR administration is as or even more effective than class room setting courses, which takes days or hours to complete.
            <em>
             Published in
             <strong>
              USA Today
             </strong>
             ,
             <a class="visited_hyperlink" href="http://www.usatoday.com/news/health/2005-11-14-cpr-fast-class_x.htm" target="_blank">
              click here to read the full article
             </a>
            </em>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </td>
        </tr>
